This is currently called from the 'main' thread, which also\n   137→// handles 'push' requests and close - the code will eventually call the 'push' code, and it needs more mutex\n   138→// protection. Original code avoided the mutexes by doing both 'push' and 'process requests' in same thread.\n   139→func (s *DiscoveryServer) processRequest(req *discovery.DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection) error {\n   140→\tstype := v3.GetShortType(req.TypeUrl)\n   141→\tlog.Debugf(\"ADS:%s: REQ %s resources:%d nonce:%s version:%s \", stype,\n   142→\t\tcon.ID(), len(req.ResourceNames), req.ResponseNonce, req.VersionInfo)\n   143→\tif req.TypeUrl == v3.HealthInfoType {\n   144→\t\ts.handleWorkloadHealthcheck(con.proxy, req)\n   145→\t\treturn nil\n   146→\t}\n   147→\n   148→\t// For now, don't let xDS piggyback debug requests start watchers.\n   149→\tif strings.HasPrefix(req.TypeUrl, v3.DebugType) {\n   150→\t\treturn s.pushXds(con,\n   151→\t\t\t&model.WatchedResource{TypeUrl: req.TypeUrl, ResourceNames: sets.New(req.ResourceNames...)},\n   152→\t\t\t&model.PushRequest{Full: true, Push: con.proxy.LastPushContext, Forced: true})\n   153→\t}\n   154→\n   155→\tshouldRespond, delta := xds.ShouldRespond(con.proxy, con.ID(), req)\n   156→\tif !shouldRespond {\n   157→\t\treturn nil\n   158→\t}\n   159→\n   160→\trequest := &model.PushRequest{\n   161→\t\tFull:   true,\n   162→\t\tPush:   con.proxy.LastPushContext,\n   163→\t\tReason: model.NewReasonStats(model.ProxyRequest),\n   164→\n   165→\t\t// The usage of LastPushTime (rather than time.Now()), is critical here for correctness; This time\n   166→\t\t// is used by the XDS cache to determine if a entry is stale. If we use Now() with an old push context,\n   167→\t\t// we may end up overriding active cache entries with stale ones.\n   168→\t\tStart:  con.proxy.LastPushTime,\n   169→\t\tDelta:  delta,\n   170→\t\tForced: true,\n   171→\t}\n   172→\n   173→\t// SidecarScope for the proxy may not have been updated based on this pushContext.\n   174→\t// It can happen when `processRequest` comes after push context has been updated(s.initPushContext),\n   175→\t// but proxy's SidecarScope has been updated(s.computeProxyState -> SetSidecarScope) due to optimizations that skip sidecar scope\n   176→\t// computation.\n   177→\tif con.proxy.SidecarScope != nil && con.proxy.SidecarScope.Version != request.Push.PushVersion {\n   178→\t\ts.computeProxyState(con.proxy, request)\n   179→\t}\n   180→\treturn s.pushXds(con, con.proxy.GetWatchedResource(req.TypeUrl), request)\n   181→}\n   182→\n   183→// StreamAggregatedResources implements the ADS interface.\n   184→func (s *DiscoveryServer) StreamAggregatedResources(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n   185→\treturn s.Stream(stream)\n   186→}\n   187→\n   188→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n   189→\tif knativeEnv != \"\" && firstRequest.Load() {\n   190→\t\t// How scaling works in knative is the first request is the \"loading\" request. During\n   191→\t\t// loading request, concurrency=1. Once that request is done, concurrency is enabled.\n   192→\t\t// However, the XDS stream is long lived, so the first request would block all others. As a\n   193→\t\t// result, we should exit the first request immediately; clients will retry.\n   194→\t\tfirstRequest.Store(false)\n   195→\t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unavailable, \"server warmup not complete; try again\")\n   196→\t}\n   197→\t// Check if server is ready to accept clients and process new requests.\n   198→\t// Currently ready means caches have been synced and hence can build\n   199→\t// clusters correctly. Without this check, InitContext() call below would\n   200→\t// initialize with empty config, leading to reconnected Envoys losing\n   201→\t// configuration. This is an additional safety check inaddition to adding\n   202→\t// cachesSynced logic to readiness probe to handle cases where kube-proxy\n   203→\t// ip tables update latencies.\n   204→\t// See https://github.com/istio/istio/issues/25495.\n   205→\tif !s.IsServerReady() {\n   206→\t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unavailable, \"server is not ready to serve discovery information\")\n   207→\t}\n   208→\n   209→\tctx := stream.Context()\n   210→\tpeerAddr := \"0.0.0.0\"\n   211→\tif peerInfo, ok := peer.FromContext(ctx); ok {\n   212→\t\tpeerAddr = peerInfo.Addr.String()\n   213→\t}\n   214→\n   215→\tif err := s.WaitForRequestLimit(stream.Context()); err != nil {\n   216→\t\tlog.Warnf(\"ADS: %q exceeded rate limit: %v\", peerAddr, err)\n   217→\t\treturn status.Errorf(codes.ResourceExhausted, \"request rate limit exceeded: %v\", err)\n   218→\t}\n   219→\n   220→\tids, err := s.authenticate(ctx)\n   221→\tif err != nil {\n   222→\t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unauthenticated, err.Error())\n   223→\t}\n   224→\tif ids != nil {\n   225→\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Authenticated XDS: %v with identity %v\", peerAddr, ids)\n   226→\t} else {\n   227→\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Unauthenticated XDS: %s\", peerAddr)\n   228→\t}\n   229→\n   230→\t// InitContext returns immediately if the context was already initialized.\n   231→\ts.globalPushContext().InitContext(s.Env, nil, nil)\n   232→\tcon := newConnection(peerAddr, stream)\n   233→\tcon.ids = ids\n   234→\tcon.s = s\n   235→\treturn xds.Stream(con)\n   236→}\n   237→\n   238→// update the node associated with the connection, after receiving a packet from envoy, also adds the connection\n   239→// to the tracking map.\n   240→func (s *DiscoveryServer) initConnection(node *core.Node, con *Connection, identities []string) error {\n   241→\t// Setup the initial proxy metadata\n   242→\tproxy, err := s.initProxyMetadata(node)\n   243→\tif err != nil {\n   244→\t\treturn err\n   245→\t}\n   246→\t// Check if proxy cluster has an alias configured, if yes use that as cluster ID for this proxy.\n   247→\tif alias, exists := s.ClusterAliases[proxy.Metadata.ClusterID]; exists {\n   248→\t\tproxy.Metadata.ClusterID = alias\n   249→\t}\n   250→\t// To ensure push context is monotonically increasing, setup LastPushContext before we addCon. This\n   251→\t// way only new push contexts will be registered for this proxy.\n   252→\tproxy.LastPushContext = s.globalPushContext()\n   253→\t// First request so initialize connection id and start tracking it.\n   254→\tcon.SetID(connectionID(proxy.ID))\n   255→\tcon.node = node\n   256→\tcon.proxy = proxy\n   257→\tif proxy.IsZTunnel() && !features.EnableAmbient {\n   258→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"ztunnel requires PILOT_ENABLE_AMBIENT=true\")\n   259→\t}\n   260→\n   261→\t// Authorize xds clients\n   262→\tif err := s.authorize(con, identities); err != nil {\n   263→\t\treturn err\n   264→\t}\n   265→\n   266→\t// Register the connection. this allows pushes to be triggered for the proxy. Note: the timing of\n   267→\t// this and initializeProxy important. While registering for pushes *after* initialization is complete seems like\n   268→\t// a better choice, it introduces a race condition; If we complete initialization of a new push\n   269→\t// context between initializeProxy and addCon, we would not get any pushes triggered for the new\n   270→\t// push context, leading the proxy to have a stale state until the next full push.\n   271→\ts.addCon(con.ID(), con)\n   272→\t// Register that initialization is complete. This triggers to calls that it is safe to access the\n   273→\t// proxy\n   274→\tdefer con.MarkInitialized()\n   275→\n   276→\t// Complete full initialization of the proxy\n   277→\tif err := s.initializeProxy(con); err != nil {\n   278→\t\ts.closeConnection(con)\n   279→\t\treturn err\n   280→\t}\n   281→\treturn nil\n   282→}\n   283→\n   284→func (s *DiscoveryServer) closeConnection(con *Connection) {\n   285→\tif con.ID() == \"\" {\n   286→\t\treturn\n   287→\t}\n   288→\ts.removeCon(con.ID())\n   289→\ts.WorkloadEntryController.OnDisconnect(con)\n   290→}\n   291→\n   292→func connectionID(node string) string {\n   293→\tid := atomic.AddInt64(&connectionNumber, 1)\n   294→\treturn node + \"-\" + strconv.FormatInt(id, 10)\n   295→}\n   296→\n   297→// initProxyMetadata initializes just the basic metadata of a proxy. The service registries have the best access to\n   319→\t// locality information, as they can read from various sources (Node on Kubernetes, for example). They will take this\n   320→\t// information and add it to the labels. We do support a (mostly undocumented/internal)\n   349→\t\t// label to override the locality, so respect that here as well.\n   350→\t\tlocalityLabel := pm.GetLocalityLabel(proxy.Labels)\n   351→\t\tif localityLabel != \"\" {\n   352→\t\t\treturn util.ConvertLocality(localityLabel)\n   353→\t\t}\n   354→\t\treturn nil\n   355→\t}\n   356→\treturn &core.Locality{\n   357→\t\tRegion:  region,\n   358→\t\tZone:    zone,\n   359→\t\tSubZone: subzone,\n   360→\t}\n   361→}\n   362→\n   363→// initializeProxy completes the initialization of a proxy. := proxy.LastPushContext\n   412→\tif request == nil {\n   413→\t\tshouldResetSidecarScope = true\n   414→\t} else {\n   415→\t\tpush = request.Push\n   416→\t\tif request.Forced {\n   417→\t\t\tshouldResetSidecarScope = true\n   418→\t\t}\n   419→\t\tfor conf := range request.ConfigsUpdated {\n   420→\t\t\tswitch conf.Kind {\n   421→\t\t\tcase kind.ServiceEntry, kind.DestinationRule, kind.VirtualService, kind.Sidecar:\n   422→\t\t\t\tshouldResetSidecarScope = true\n   423→\t\t\tcase kind.Gateway:\n   424→\t\t\t\tshouldResetGateway = true\n   425→\t\t\tcase 430→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   431→\t\t\t}\n   432→\t\t}\n   433→\t}\n   434→\t// compute the sidecarscope for both proxy type whenever it changes.\n   435→\tif shouldResetSidecarScope {\n net.Listen(adsNetwork, adsAddress)\n   214→\tif err != nil {\n   215→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to listen: %w\", err)\n   216→\t}\n   217→\n   218→\t// register services\n   219→\tv3discovery.RegisterAggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer(grpcServer, serverv3)\n   220→\tv3endpoint.RegisterEndpointDiscoveryServiceServer(grpcServer, serverv3)\n   221→\tv3cluster.RegisterClusterDiscoveryServiceServer(grpcServer, serverv3)\n   222→\tv3route.RegisterRouteDiscoveryServiceServer(grpcServer, serverv3)\n   223→\tv3listener.RegisterListenerDiscoveryServiceServer(grpcServer, serverv3)\n   224→\n   225→\tdlog.Infof(ctx, \"Listening on %s:%s\", adsNetwork, adsAddress)\n   226→\n   227→\tsc := &dhttp.ServerConfig{\n   228→\t\tHandler: grpcServer,\n   229→\t}\n   230→\treturn sc.Serve(ctx, lis)\n   231→}\n   232→\n   233→// Decoders for unmarshalling our config\n   234→var decoders = map[string](func([]byte, proto.Message) error){\n   235→\t\".json\": protojson.Unmarshal,\n   236→\t\".pb\":   prototext.Unmarshal,\n   237→}\n   238→\n   239→func isDecodable(name string) bool {\n   240→\tif strings.HasPrefix(name, \".\") {\n   241→\t\treturn false\n   242→\t}\n   243→\n   244→\text := filepath.Ext(name)\n   245→\t_, ok := decoders[ext]\n   246→\treturn ok\n   247→}\n   248→\n   249→// Not sure if there is a better way to do this, but we cast to this\n   250→// so we can call the generated Validate method.\n   251→type Validatable interface {\n   252→\tproto.Message\n   253→\tValidate() error\n   254→}\n   255→\n   256→func Decode(ctx context.Context, name string) (proto.Message, error) {\n   257→\tany := &anypb.Any{}\n   258→\tcontents, err := ioutil.ReadFile(name)\n   259→\tif err != nil {\n   260→\t\treturn nil, err\n   261→\t}\n   262→\n   263→\text := filepath.Ext(name)\n   264→\tdecoder := decoders[ext]\n   265→\terr = decoder(contents, any)\n   266→\tif err != nil {\n   267→\t\treturn nil, err\n   268→\t}\n   269→\n   270→\tm, err := any.UnmarshalNew()\n   271→\tif err != nil {\n   272→\t\treturn nil, err\n   273→\t}\n   274→\n   275→\tv := m.(Validatable)\n   276→\n   277→\tif err := v.Validate(); err != nil {\n   278→\t\treturn nil, err\n   279→\t}\n   280→\tdlog.Infof(ctx, \"Loaded file %s\", name)\n   281→\treturn v, nil\n   282→}\n   283→\n   284→// Observability:\n   285→//\n   286→// These \"expanded\" snapshots make the snapshots we log easier to read: basically,\n   287→// instead of just indexing by Golang types, make the JSON marshal with real names.\n   288→type v3ExpandedSnapshot struct {\n   289→\tEndpoints ecp_v3_cache.Resources `json:\"endpoints\"`\n   290→\tClusters  ecp_v3_cache.Resources `json:\"clusters\"`\n   291→\tRoutes    ecp_v3_cache.Resources `json:\"routes\"`\n   292→\tListeners ecp_v3_cache.Resources `json:\"listeners\"`\n   293→\tRuntimes  ecp_v3_cache.Resources `json:\"runtimes\"`\n   294→}\n   295→\n   296→func NewV3ExpandedSnapshot(v3snap *ecp_v3_cache.Snapshot) v3ExpandedSnapshot {\n   297→\treturn v3ExpandedSnapshot{\n   298→\t\tEndpoints: v3snap.Resources[ecp_cache_types.Endpoint],\n   299→\t\tClusters:  v3snap.Resources[ecp_cache_types.Cluster],\n   300→\t\tRoutes:    v3snap.Resources[ecp_cache_types.Route],\n   301→\t\tListeners: v3snap.Resources[ecp_cache_types.Listener],\n   302→\t\tRuntimes:  v3snap.Resources[ecp_cache_types.Runtime],\n   303→\t}\n   304→}\n   305→\n   306→// A combinedSnapshot has both a V2 and V3 snapshot, for logging.\n   307→type combinedSnapshot struct {\n   308→\tVersion string             `json:\"version\"`\n   309→\tV3      v3ExpandedSnapshot `json:\"v3\"`\n   310→}\n   311→\n   312→// csDump creates a combinedSnapshot from a V2 snapshot and a V3 snapshot, then\n   313→// dumps the combinedSnapshot to disk. Only numsnaps snapshots are kept: ambex-1.json\n   314→// is the newest, then ambex-2.json, etc., so ambex-$numsnaps.json is the oldest.\n   315→// Every time we write a new one, we rename all the older ones, ditching the oldest\n   316→// after we've written numsnaps snapshots.\n   317→func csDump(ctx context.Context, snapdirPath string, numsnaps int, generation int, v3snap *ecp_v3_cache.Snapshot) {\n   318→\tif numsnaps <= 0 {\n   319→\t\t// Don't do snapshotting at all.\n   320→\t\treturn\n   321→\t}\n   322→\n   323→\t// OK, they want snapshots. Make a proper version string...\n   324→\tversion := fmt.Sprintf(\"v%d\", generation)\n   325→\n   326→\t// ...and a combinedSnapshot.\n   327→\tcs := combinedSnapshot{\n   328→\t\tVersion: version,\n   329→\t\tV3:      NewV3ExpandedSnapshot(v3snap),\n   330→\t}\n   331→\n   332→\t// Next up, marshal as JSON and write to ambex-0.json. Note that we\n   333→\t// didn't say anything about a -0 file; that's because it's about to\n   334→\t// be renamed.\n   335→\n   336→\tbs, err := json.MarshalIndent(cs, \"\", \"  \")\n   337→\n   338→\tif err != nil {\n   339→\t\tdlog.Errorf(ctx, \"CSNAP: marshal failure: %s\", err)\n   340→\t\treturn\n   341→\t}\n   342→\n   343→\tcsPath := path.Join(snapdirPath, \"ambex-0.json\")\n   344→\n   345→\terr = ioutil.WriteFile(csPath, bs, 0644)\n   346→\n   347→\tif err != nil {\n   348→\t\tdlog.Errorf(ctx, \"CSNAP: write failure: %s\", err)\n   349→\t} else {\n   350→\t\tdlog.Infof(ctx, \"Saved snapshot %s\", version)\n   351→\t}\n   352→\n   353→\t// Rotate everything one file down. This includes renaming the just-written\n   354→\t// ambex-0 to ambex-1.\n   355→\tfor i := numsnaps; i > 0; i-- {\n   356→\t\tprevious := i - 1\n   357→\n   358→\t\tfromPath := path.Join(snapdirPath, fmt.Sprintf(\"ambex-%d.json\", previous))\n   359→\t\ttoPath := path.Join(snapdirPath, fmt.Sprintf(\"ambex-%d.json\", i))\n   360→\n   361→\t\terr := os.Rename(fromPath, toPath)\n   362→\n   363→\t\tif (err != nil) && !os.IsNotExist(err) {\n   364→\t\t\tdlog.Infof(ctx, \"CSNAP: could not rename %s -> %s: %#v\", fromPath, toPath, err)\n   365→\t\t}\n   366→\t}\n   367→}\n   368→\n   369→// Get an updated snapshot going.\n   370→func update(\n   371→\tctx context.Context,\n   372→\tsnapdirPath string,\n   373→\tnumsnaps int,\n   374→\tedsBypass bool,\n   375→\tconfigv3 ecp_v3_cache.SnapshotCache,\n   376→\tgeneration *int,\n   377→\tdirs []string,\n   378→\tedsEndpointsV3 map[string]*v3endpointconfig.ClusterLoadAssignment,\n   379→\tfastpathSnapshot *FastpathSnapshot,\n   380→\tupdates chan<- Update,\n   381→) error {\n   382→\n   383→\tclustersv3 := []ecp_cache_types.Resource{}  // v3.Cluster\n   384→\troutesv3 := []ecp_cache_types.Resource{}    // v3.RouteConfiguration\n   385→\tlistenersv3 := []ecp_cache_types.Resource{} // v3.Listener\n   386→\truntimesv3 := []ecp_cache_types.Resource{}  // v3.Runtime\n   387→\n   388→\tvar filenames []string\n   389→\n   390→\tfor _, dir := range dirs {\n   391→\t\tfiles, err := ioutil.ReadDir(dir)\n   392→\t\tif err != nil {\n   393→\t\t\tdlog.Warnf(ctx, \"Error listing %q: %v\", dir, err)\n   394→\t\t\tcontinue\n   395→\t\t}\n   396→\t\tfor _, file := range files {\n   397→\t\t\tname := file.Name()\n   398→\t\t\tif isDecodable(name) {\n   399→\t\t\t\tfilenames = append(filenames, filepath.Join(dir, name))\n   400→\t\t\t}\n   401→\t\t}\n   402→\t}\n   403→\n   404→\tfor _, name := range filenames {\n   405→\t\tm, e := Decode(ctx, name)\n   406→\t\tif e != nil {\n   407→\t\t\tdlog.Warnf(ctx, \"%s: %v\", name, e)\n   408→\t\t\tcontinue\n   409→\t\t}\n   410→\t\tvar dst *[]ecp_cache_types.Resource\n   411→\t\tswitch m.(type) {\n   412→\t\tcase *v3clusterconfig.Cluster:\n   413→\t\t\tdst = &clustersv3\n   414→\t\tcase *v3routeconfig.RouteConfiguration:\n   415→\t\t\tdst = &routesv3\n   416→\t\tcase *v3listenerconfig.Listener:\n   417→\t\t\tdst = &listenersv3\n   418→\t\tcase *v3runtime.Runtime:\n   419→\t\t\tdst = &runtimesv3\n   420→\t\tcase *v3bootstrap.Bootstrap:\n   421→\t\t\tbs := m.(*v3bootstrap.Bootstrap)\n   422→\t\t\tsr := bs.StaticResources\n   423→\t\t\tfor _, lst := range sr.Listeners {\n   424→\t\t\t\t// When the RouteConfiguration is embedded in the listener, it will cause envoy to\n   425→\t\t\t\t// go through a complete drain cycle whenever there is a routing change and that\n   426→\t\t\t\t// will potentially disrupt in-flight requests. By converting all listeners to use\n   427→\t\t\t\t// RDS rather than inlining their routing configuration, we significantly reduce the\n   428→\t\t\t\t// set of circumstances where the listener definition itself changes, and this in\n   429→\t\t\t\t// turn reduces the set of circumstances where envoy has to go through that drain\n   430→\t\t\t\t// process and disrupt in-flight requests.\n   431→\t\t\t\trdsListener, routeConfigs, err := V3ListenerToRdsListener(lst)\n   432→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   433→\t\t\t\t\tdlog.Errorf(ctx, \"Error converting listener to RDS: %+v\", err)\n   434→\t\t\t\t\tlistenersv3 = append(listenersv3, proto.Clone(lst).(ecp_cache_types.Resource))\n   435→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   436→\t\t\t\t}\n   437→\t\t\t\tlistenersv3 = append(listenersv3, rdsListener)\n   438→\t\t\t\tfor _, rc := range routeConfigs {\n   439→\t\t\t\t\t// These routes will get included in the configuration snapshot created below.\n   440→\t\t\t\t\troutesv3 = append(routesv3, rc)\n   441→\t\t\t\t}\n   442→\t\t\t}\n   443→\t\t\tfor _, cls := range sr.Clusters {\n   444→\t\t\t\tclustersv3 = append(clustersv3, proto.Clone(cls).(ecp_cache_types.Resource))\n   445→\t\t\t}\n   446→\t\t\tcontinue\n   447→\t\tdefault:\n   448→\t\t\tdlog.Warnf(ctx, \"Unrecognized resource %s: %v\", name, e)\n   449→\t\t\tcontinue\n   450→\t\t}\n   451→\t\t*dst = append(*dst, m.(ecp_cache_types.Resource))\n   452→\t}\n   453→\n   454→\tif fastpathSnapshot != nil && fastpathSnapshot.Snapshot != nil {\n   455→\t\tfor _, lst := range fastpathSnapshot.Snapshot.Resources[ecp_cache_types.Listener].Items {\n   456→\t\t\tlistenersv3 = append(listenersv3, lst.Resource)\n   457→\t\t}\n   458→\t\tfor _, route := range fastpathSnapshot.Snapshot.Resources[ecp_cache_types.Route].Items {\n   459→\t\t\troutesv3 = append(routesv3, route.Resource)\n   460→\t\t}\n   461→\t\tfor _, clu := range fastpathSnapshot.Snapshot.Resources[ecp_cache_types.Cluster].Items {\n   462→\t\t\tclustersv3 = append(clustersv3, clu.Resource)\n   463→\t\t}\n   464→\t\t// We intentionally omit endpoints since those are carried separately.\n   465→\t}\n   466→\n   467→\t// The configuration data that reaches us here arrives via two parallel paths that race each\n   468→\t// other. The endpoint data comes in realtime directly from the golang watcher in the entrypoint\n   469→\t// package. The cluster configuration comes from the python code. Either one can win which means\n   470→\t// we might at times see endpoint data with no corresponding cluster and we might also see\n   471→\t// clusters with no corresponding endpoint data. Both of these circumstances should be\n   472→\t// transient.\n   473→\t//\n   474→\t// To produce a consistent configuration we do an outer join operation on the endpoint and\n   475→\t// cluster configuration that we have at this moment. If there is no endpoint information for a\n   476→\t// given cluster, we will synthesize an empty ClusterLoadAssignment.\n   477→\t//\n   478→\t// Note that a cluster not existing is very different to envoy than a cluster existing but\n   479→\t// having an empty ClusterLoadAssignment. When envoy first discovers clusters it goes through a\n   480→\t// warmup process to be sure the cluster is properly bootstrapped before routing traffic to\n   481→\t// it. See here for more details:\n   482→\t//\n   483→\t// https://www.envoyproxy.io/docs/envoy/latest/intro/arch_overview/upstream/cluster_manager.html?highlight=cluster%20warming\n   484→\t//\n   485→\t// For this reason if there is no endpoint data for the cluster we will synthesize an empty\n   486→\t// ClusterLoadAssignment rather than filtering out the cluster. This avoids triggering the\n   487→\t// warmup sequence in scenarios where the endpoint data for a cluster is really flapping into\n   488→\t// and out of existence. In that circumstance we want to faithfully relay to envoy that the\n   489→\t// cluster exists but currently has no endpoints.\n   490→\tendpointsv3 := JoinEdsClustersV3(ctx, clustersv3, edsEndpointsV3, edsBypass)\n   491→\n   492→\t// Create a new configuration snapshot from everything we have just loaded from disk.\n   493→\tcurgen := *generation\n   494→\t*generation++\n   495→\n   496→\tversion := fmt.Sprintf(\"v%d\", curgen)\n   497→\n   498→\tsnapshotResources := map[ecp_v3_resource.Type][]ecp_cache_types.Resource{\n   499→\t\tecp_v3_resource.EndpointType: endpointsv3,\n   500→\t\tecp_v3_resource.ClusterType:  clustersv3,\n   501→\t\tecp_v3_resource.RouteType:    routesv3,\n   502→\t\tecp_v3_resource.ListenerType: listenersv3,\n   503→\t\tecp_v3_resource.RuntimeType:  runtimesv3,\n   504→\t}\n   505→\n   506→\tsnapshot, err := ecp_v3_cache.NewSnapshot(version, snapshotResources)\n   507→\tif err != nil {\n   508→\t\tdlog.Errorf(ctx, \"V3 Snapshot error: %v\", err)\n   509→\t\treturn nil // TODO: should we return the error, rather than just logging it?\n   510→\t}\n   511→\n   512→\tif err := snapshot.Consistent(); err != nil {\n   513→\t\tbs, _ := json.Marshal(snapshot)\n   514→\t\tdlog.Errorf(ctx, \"V3 Snapshot inconsistency: %v: %s\", err, bs)\n   515→\t\treturn nil // TODO: should we return the error, rather than just logging it?\n   516→\t}\n   517→\n   518→\t// This used to just directly update envoy. Since we want ratelimiting, we now send an\n   519→\t// Update object down the channel with a function that knows how to do the update if/when\n   520→\t// the ratelimiting logic decides.\n   521→\n   522→\tdlog.Debugf(ctx, \"Created snapshot %s\", version)\n   523→\tcsDump(ctx, snapdirPath, numsnaps, curgen, snapshot)\n   524→\n   525→\tupdate := Update{version, func() error {\n   526→\t\tdlog.Debugf(ctx, \"Accepting snapshot %s\", version)\n   527→\n   528→\t\terr = configv3.SetSnapshot(ctx, \"test-id\", snapshot)\n   529→\t\tif err != nil {\n   530→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"v3 Snapshot error %q for %+v\", err, snapshot)\n   531→\t\t}\n   532→\n   533→\t\treturn nil\n   534→\t}}\n   535→\n   536→\t// We also need to pay attention to contexts here so we can shutdown properly. If we didn't\n   537→\t// have the context portion, the ratelimit goroutine could shutdown first and we could end\n   538→\t// up blocking here and never shutting down.\n   539→\tselect {\n   540→\tcase updates <- update:\n   541→\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   542→\t}\n   543→\treturn nil\n   544→}\n   545→\n   546→type logAdapterBase struct {\n   547→\tprefix string\n   548→}\n   549→type logAdapterV3 struct {\n   550→\tlogAdapterBase\n   551→}\n   552→\n   553→var _ ecp_v3_server.Callbacks = logAdapterV3{}\n   554→var _ ecp_log.Logger = logAdapterV3{}\n   555→\n   556→// Debugf implements ecp_log.Logger.\n   557→func (l logAdapterBase) Debugf(format string, args ...interface{}) {\n   558→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), format, args...)\n   559→}\n   560→\n   561→// Infof implements ecp_log.Logger.\n   562→func (l logAdapterBase) Infof(format string, args ...interface{}) {\n   563→\tdlog.Infof(context.TODO(), format, args...)\n   564→}\n   565→\n   566→// Warnf implements ecp_log.Logger.\n   567→func (l logAdapterBase) Warnf(format string, args ...interface{}) {\n   568→\tdlog.Warnf(context.TODO(), format, args...)\n   569→}\n   570→\n   571→// Errorf implements ecp_log.Logger.\n   572→func (l logAdapterBase) Errorf(format string, args ...interface{}) {\n   573→\tdlog.Errorf(context.TODO(), format, args...)\n   574→}\n   575→\n   576→// OnStreamOpen implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   577→func (l logAdapterBase) OnStreamOpen(ctx context.Context, sid int64, stype string) error {\n   578→\tdlog.Debugf(ctx, \"%v Stream open[%v]: %v\", l.prefix, sid, stype)\n   579→\treturn nil\n   580→}\n   581→\n   582→// OnStreamClosed implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   583→func (l logAdapterBase) OnStreamClosed(sid int64, node *v3core.Node) {\n   584→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), \"%v Stream closed[%v]\", l.prefix, sid)\n   585→}\n   586→\n   587→// OnStreamRequest implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   588→func (l logAdapterV3) OnStreamRequest(sid int64, req *v3discovery.DiscoveryRequest) error {\n   589→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), \"V3 Stream request[%v] for type %s: requesting %d resources\", sid, req.TypeUrl, len(req.ResourceNames))\n   590→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), \"V3 Stream request[%v] dump: %v\", sid, req)\n   591→\treturn nil\n   592→}\n   593→\n   594→// OnStreamResponse implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   595→func (l logAdapterV3) OnStreamResponse(ctx context.Context, sid int64, req *v3discovery.DiscoveryRequest, res *v3discovery.DiscoveryResponse) {\n   596→\tdlog.Debugf(ctx, \"V3 Stream response[%v] for type %s: returning %d resources\", sid, res.TypeUrl, len(res.Resources))\n   597→\tdlog.Debugf(ctx, \"V3 Stream dump response[%v]: %v -> %v\", sid, req, res)\n   598→}\n   599→\n   600→// OnDeltaStreamOpen implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   601→func (l logAdapterV3) OnDeltaStreamOpen(ctx context.Context, sid int64, stype string) error {\n   602→\tdlog.Debugf(ctx, \"%v DeltaStream open[%v]: %v\", l.prefix, sid, stype)\n   603→\treturn nil\n   604→}\n   605→\n   606→// OnDeltaStreamClosed implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   607→func (l logAdapterV3) OnDeltaStreamClosed(sid int64, node *v3core.Node) {\n   608→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), \"%v DeltaStream closed[%v]\", l.prefix, sid)\n   609→}\n   610→\n   611→// OnStreamDeltaRequest implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   612→func (l logAdapterV3) OnStreamDeltaRequest(sid int64, req *v3discovery.DeltaDiscoveryRequest) error {\n   613→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), \"V3 Stream DeltaRequest[%v] for type %s: subscribing for %d resources\", sid, req.TypeUrl, len(req.ResourceNamesSubscribe))\n   614→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), \"V3 Stream DeltaRequest[%v] dump: %v\", sid, req)\n   615→\treturn nil\n   616→}\n   617→\n   618→// OnStreamDelatResponse implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   619→func (l logAdapterV3) OnStreamDeltaResponse(sid int64, req *v3discovery.DeltaDiscoveryRequest, res *v3discovery.DeltaDiscoveryResponse) {\n   620→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), \"V3 Stream dump DeltaResponse[%v] for type %s: returning %d resources\", sid, res.TypeUrl, len(res.Resources))\n   621→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), \"V3 Stream dump DeltaResponse[%v]: %v -> %v\", sid, req, res)\n   622→}\n   623→\n   624→// OnFetchRequest implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   625→func (l logAdapterV3) OnFetchRequest(ctx context.Context, r *v3discovery.DiscoveryRequest) error {\n   626→\tdlog.Debugf(ctx, \"V3 Fetch request: %v\", r)\n   627→\treturn nil\n   628→}\n   629→\n   630→// OnFetchResponse implements ecp_v3_server.Callbacks.\n   631→func (l logAdapterV3) OnFetchResponse(req *v3discovery.DiscoveryRequest, res *v3discovery.DiscoveryResponse) {\n   632→\tdlog.Debugf(context.TODO(), \"V3 Fetch response: %v -> %v\", req, res)\n   633→}\n   634→\n   635→func Main(\n   636→\tctx context.Context,\n   637→\tVersion string,\n   638→\tgetUsage MemoryGetter,\n   639→\tfastpathCh <-chan *FastpathSnapshot,\n   640→\trawArgs ...string,\n   641→) error {\n   642→\targs, err := parseArgs(ctx, rawArgs...)\n   643→\tif err != nil {\n   644→\t\treturn err\n   645→\t}\n   646→\n   647→\tdlog.Infof(ctx, \"Ambex %s starting, snapdirPath %s\", Version, args.snapdirPath)\n   648→\n   649→\twatcher, err := fsnotify.NewWatcher()\n   650→\tif err != nil {\n   651→\t\treturn err\n   652→\t}\n   653→\tdefer watcher.Close()\n   654→\n   655→\tif args.watch {\n   656→\t\tfor _, d := range args.dirs {\n   657→\t\t\tif err := watcher.Add(d); err != nil {\n   658→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   659→\t\t\t}\n   660→\t\t}\n   661→\t}\n   662→\n   663→\t// The golang signal package does not block when it writes to the channel. We therefore need a\n   664→\t// nonzero buffer for the channel to minimize the possiblity that we miss out on a signal that\n   665→\t// comes in while we are doing work and not reading from the channel. To minimize the chance\n   666→\t// of that happening we will choose a buffer size of 100. This is currently called from the 'main' thread, which also\n   137→// handles 'push' requests and close - the code will eventually call the 'push' code, and it needs more mutex\n   138→// protection. Original code avoided the mutexes by doing both 'push' and 'process requests' in same thread.\n   139→func (s *DiscoveryServer) processRequest(req *discovery.DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection) error {\n   140→\tstype := v3.GetShortType(req.TypeUrl)\n   141→\tlog.Debugf(\"ADS:%s: REQ %s resources:%d nonce:%s version:%s \", stype,\n   142→\t\tcon.ID(), len(req.ResourceNames), req.ResponseNonce, req.VersionInfo)\n   143→\tif req.TypeUrl == v3.HealthInfoType {\n   144→\t\ts.handleWorkloadHealthcheck(con.proxy, req)\n   145→\t\treturn nil\n   146→\t}\n   147→\n   148→\t// For now, don't let xDS piggyback debug requests start watchers.\n   149→\tif strings.HasPrefix(req.TypeUrl, v3.DebugType) {\n   150→\t\treturn s.pushXds(con,\n   151→\t\t\t&model.WatchedResource{TypeUrl: req.TypeUrl, ResourceNames: sets.New(req.ResourceNames...)},\n   152→\t\t\t&model.PushRequest{Full: true, Push: con.proxy.LastPushContext, Forced: true})\n   153→\t}\n   154→\n   155→\tshouldRespond, delta := xds.ShouldRespond(con.proxy, con.ID(), req)\n   156→\tif !shouldRespond {\n   157→\t\treturn nil\n   158→\t}\n   159→\n   160→\trequest := &model.PushRequest{\n   161→\t\tFull:   true,\n   162→\t\tPush:   con.proxy.LastPushContext,\n   163→\t\tReason: model.NewReasonStats(model.ProxyRequest),\n   164→\n   165→\t\t// The usage of LastPushTime (rather than time.Now()), is critical here for correctness; This time\n   166→\t\t// is used by the XDS cache to determine if a entry is stale. If we use Now() with an old push context,\n   167→\t\t// we may end up overriding active cache entries with stale ones.\n   168→\t\tStart:  con.proxy.LastPushTime,\n   169→\t\tDelta:  delta,\n   170→\t\tForced: true,\n   171→\t}\n   172→\n   173→\t// SidecarScope for the proxy may not have been updated based on this pushContext.\n   174→\t// It can happen when `processRequest` comes after push context has been updated(s.initPushContext),\n   175→\t// but proxy's SidecarScope has been updated(s.computeProxyState -> SetSidecarScope) due to optimizations that skip sidecar scope\n   176→\t// computation.\n   177→\tif con.proxy.SidecarScope != nil && con.proxy.SidecarScope.Version != request.Push.PushVersion {\n   178→\t\ts.computeProxyState(con.proxy, request)\n   179→\t}\n   180→\treturn s.pushXds(con, con.proxy.GetWatchedResource(req.TypeUrl), request)\n   181→}\n   182→\n   183→// StreamAggregatedResources implements the ADS interface.\n   184→func (s *DiscoveryServer) StreamAggregatedResources(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n   185→\treturn s.Stream(stream)\n   186→}\n   187→\n   188→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n   189→\tif knativeEnv != \"\" && firstRequest.Load() {\n   190→\t\t// How scaling works in knative is the first request is the \"loading\" request. *     of the methods in a callback object.\n * - Once the Server is running, Envoy can open a gRPC stream to it.\n *   - On connection, Envoy will get handed the most recent Snapshot that\n *     the
